###House Lannister####
#####Hear me Roar#####

#Lannisters Ancient History.
#Just updated some things. I got to a chapter in AFoC were Jaime is speaking to his aunt. It's stated that Tytos was third-born.
#So rather than mess with his younger brothers Damon (Joanna's dad) and Damion (Lannisport Lannisters).
#I've added two elder brothers to them all, who died childless. Added random wives for Damon so Tybolt and Tya are full siblings and one to Tybolt so his five sons are full blooded too.

###A Lannister always pays his debt###
###Lann the Clever, founder of House Lannister###
